data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contexto do Projeto (humano) — Tradutor LLM</h1><a id="user-content-contexto-do-projeto-humano--tradutor-llm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contexto do Projeto (humano) — Tradutor LLM" href="#contexto-do-projeto-humano--tradutor-llm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 <blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Este documento foi montado após varredura de <code>README.md</code>, <code>tradutor/main.py</code>, <code>tradutor/translate.py</code>, <code>tradutor/refine.py</code>, <code>tradutor/cache_utils.py</code>, <code>tradutor/config.py</code> e diretórios <code>tests/</code>.
Se algo parecer incompleto, confira os arquivos acima.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arquitetura (componentes e responsabilidades)</h2><a id="user-content-arquitetura-componentes-e-responsabilidades" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arquitetura (componentes e responsabilidades)" href="#arquitetura-componentes-e-responsabilidades"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>CLI principal</strong>: <code>tradutor/main.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Subcomandos: <code>traduz</code>, <code>traduz-md</code>, <code>refina</code>, <code>pdf</code>.</li>
<li>Orquestra o pipeline e aplica flags/configs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Config</strong>: <code>tradutor/config.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Define defaults e carrega <code>config.yaml</code>.</li>
<li>Define <code>data_dir</code>, <code>output_dir</code>, modelos/temperaturas/ctx, PDF settings.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Tradução</strong>: <code>tradutor/translate.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pré-processamento, chunking, glossário por chunk, chamadas LLM, sanitização.</li>
<li>Grava métricas/report e manifesto de progresso.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Desquebrar</strong>: <code>tradutor/desquebrar.py</code>, <code>tradutor/desquebrar_safe.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Une linhas quebradas (LLM ou heurístico “safe”).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Refine</strong>: <code>tradutor/refine.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Revisão em chunks, guardrails, cleanup determinístico e pós-processo.</li>
<li>Grava métricas/report e manifesto de progresso.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>PDF</strong>: <code>tradutor/pdf.py</code>, <code>tradutor/pdf_export.py</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Exporta Markdown → PDF usando ReportLab.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Utilitários</strong>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tradutor/cache_utils.py</code> (cache por chunk), <code>tradutor/preprocess.py</code>, <code>tradutor/sanitizer.py</code> etc.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Wrappers legados</strong>: <code>tradutor.py</code>, <code>refinador.py</code>, <code>desquebrar.py</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fluxo de dados (alto nível)</h2><a id="user-content-fluxo-de-dados-alto-nível" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fluxo de dados (alto nível)" href="#fluxo-de-dados-alto-nível"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Extração</strong>: PDF → texto (<code>tradutor/pdf_reader.py</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Pré-processamento</strong>: limpeza básica + remoção de front-matter/TOC (<code>tradutor/preprocess.py</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Desquebrar</strong> (opcional): une linhas quebradas (LLM ou safe).</li>
<li><strong>Tradução</strong>: chunking + LLM + sanitização + recomposição (<code>tradutor/translate.py</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Cleanup antes do refine</strong> (opcional): heurísticas determinísticas.</li>
<li><strong>Refine</strong>: revisão por chunk com guardrails (<code>tradutor/refine.py</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Pós-processamento</strong>: correções finais e normalizadores.</li>
<li><strong>PDF</strong> (opcional): exporta <code>*_pt_refinado.md</code> → PDF.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Artefatos/JSONs principais (schemas resumidos)</h2><a id="user-content-artefatosjsons-principais-schemas-resumidos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Artefatos/JSONs principais (schemas resumidos)" href="#artefatosjsons-principais-schemas-resumidos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Campos listados abaixo foram coletados dos writers no código. Outros campos podem aparecer.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>*_translate_report.json</code> (em <code>saida/</code>)</h3><a id="user-content-_translate_reportjson-em-saida" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: *_translate_report.json (em saida/)" href="#_translate_reportjson-em-saida"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>mode</code>: <code>"translate"</code></li>
<li><code>status</code>: <code>"ok"</code> ou <code>"failed"</code></li>

<li><code>total_chunks</code>, <code>cache_hits</code>, <code>fallbacks</code>, <code>failed_chunks</code>, <code>collapse_detected</code>, <code>duplicates_reused</code></li>
<li><code>pipeline_version</code>, <code>timestamp</code></li>
<li><code>effective_translate_chunk_chars</code>, <code>max_chunk_chars_observed</code></li>
<li><code>dialogue_splits</code>, <code>triple_quotes_removed</code></li>
<li><code>paragraph_mismatch</code> (opcional)</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Debugs</h3><a id="user-content-debugs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Debugs" href="#debugs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>*_pt_chunks_debug.jsonl</code>: debug detalhado por chunk (tradução).</li>
<li><code>*_chunks_debug.jsonl</code>: debug por chunk (refine).</li>
<li><code>saida/debug_refine*/</code>: arquivos <code>orig/raw/final</code> quando <code>--debug-refine</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Debug playbook (chunks/merge/cache)</h2><a id="user-content-debug-playbook-chunksmergecache" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Debug playbook (chunks/merge/cache)" href="#debug-playbook-chunksmergecache"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Reproduzir bug de chunking</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Rode com <code>--debug-chunks</code>.</li>
<li>Inspecione <code>saida/*_pt_chunks_debug.jsonl</code> (tradução) ou <code>*_chunks_debug.jsonl</code> (refine).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Verificar cache indevido</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Limpe com <code>--clear-cache all</code> ou apague <code>saida/cache_*</code>.</li>
<li>Rode novamente e compare <code>cache_hits</code> nos reports.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Problemas de merge/recomposição</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Compare <code>*_progress.json</code> (mapa <code>chunks</code>) com o arquivo final.</li>
<li>Procure discrepâncias em <code>paragraph_mismatch</code> do report.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Saídas colapsadas ou contaminadas</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Verifique <code>collapse_detected</code> nos reports.</li>
<li>Procure entradas suspeitas nos JSONLs de debug.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">FAQ de manutenção</h2><a id="user-content-faq-de-manutenção" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: FAQ de manutenção" href="#faq-de-manutenção"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Como adicionar um novo volume?</h3><a id="user-content-como-adicionar-um-novo-volume" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Como adicionar um novo volume?" href="#como-adicionar-um-novo-volume"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Coloque o PDF em <code>data/</code>.</li>
<li>Ajuste <code>config.yaml</code> se necessário (modelos, chunk sizes, pdf settings).</li>
<li>Rode: <code>python -m tradutor.main traduz --input "data/arquivo.pdf"</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Como ajustar chunking?</h3><a id="user-content-como-ajustar-chunking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Como ajustar chunking?" href="#como-ajustar-chunking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Em <code>config.yaml</code>, ajuste <code>translate_chunk_chars</code> e/ou <code>refine_chunk_chars</code>.</li>
<li>Re-execute com <code>--clear-cache all</code> para evitar reuso de chunks antigos.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Como trocar modelo/backend?</h3><a id="user-content-como-trocar-modelobackend" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Como trocar modelo/backend?" href="#como-trocar-modelobackend"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Em <code>config.yaml</code>: <code>translate_backend</code>, <code>translate_model</code>, <code>refine_backend</code>, <code>refine_model</code>.</li>
<li>Para Gemini, configure apenas a variável <code>GEMINI_API_KEY</code> no ambiente.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Como alterar pipeline (desquebrar/refine/pdf)?</h3><a id="user-content-como-alterar-pipeline-desquebrarrefinepdf" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Como alterar pipeline (desquebrar/refine/pdf)?" href="#como-alterar-pipeline-desquebrarrefinepdf"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use flags: <code>--no-refine</code>, <code>--use-desquebrar/--no-use-desquebrar</code>, <code>--pdf-enabled</code>.</li>
<li>Para desquebrar “safe” (sem LLM): <code>--desquebrar-mode safe</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Observações de incerteza</h2><a id="user-content-observações-de-incerteza" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Observações de incerteza" href="#observações-de-incerteza"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Não encontrei configuração formal de lint/format (<code>pyproject.toml</code>, <code>setup.cfg</code>, <code>tox.ini</code>).</li>
<li>Não encontrei políticas de branch/commit. Caso existam, documente em <code>AGENTS.md</code>.</li>
</ul>
